 jaahir he aise main aapkotatkaal tikat ke bharoserahana hoga
 But there is no less fight to cut the Tatkal ticket
 lekin ghabrie nahin
 From IRCTC website, we have brought seven surefire tips for ticket deductors which will help you get confirmed Tatkal tickets
 1
 Install adblocker on your computer or laptop: First of all install adblocker on your computer or laptop
 ab aap sochenge ki iskaa tikat kataane se kya matlab, to ham aapako bataate hai
 You must have noticed that whenever you open any website through Chrome or Mozilla, many types of ads start coming automatically
 kuch aisa hi www
 irctc
 co
 also occurs in aise aid tatkaal tikat kataane ke dauraan aapke liye musiibat khadi kar sakate hai kyonki isse aapkaa samay barbaad hota he
 So it is better that such ads be blocked so that its pop ups do not bother you while cutting tickets
 2
 Use two ids: Always use two ids
 agar aapke paas IRCTC par sirf ek hi acount he to apane dost yaa rishtedaar ye ek duusare acount kaa password maang len
 Then log both ids but be aware that both ids are open on different browsers or else both of your ids will be logged out automatically and the whole game may get spoiled
 3
 Find out when the Tatkal is opening: By the way, in any train, the immediate quota opens 24 hours before
 lekin ham aapako bataa den ki agar koi train apane gantvay se khulkar duusare din aapke stesan par pahunchati he to waisi trainon kaa tatkaal kota us train ke gantvy se khulne ke 24 ghante pehle khul jaataa he
 In this case, you have 48 hours
 to tatkaal tikat lene ke pehle koshish karen ki pehle aisi trainon kaa pataa kiya jaae jisamen 48 ghante pehle tatkaal kota khulata ho
 By using this formula, you can stay in profit
 4
 Fill the passenger information first: As we know, the immediate quota opens at 10 am
 aap koshish karen ki paisanger information list ko pehle bhar len
 Because if you start this work at 10 o'clock, your time will be wasted and here, in a matter of seconds, the quota becomes full immediately
 paisanger informension list bharne ke bhi do tareeke hai
 First way: Once you go to the passenger list, fill all the information before 10 pm so that when you go to cut the ticket, all the details will automatically reflect in the drop down
 aapako bas use select karnaa hoga
 This will save you time
 doosraa tarika:ye tarika he master list kaa
 This is a facility in IRCTC where you can fill all the information beforehand
 aapako baad main bas use select karnaa hoga
 You can save many minutes by doing this
 5
 Keep all the documents ready in advance: Before getting the tickets cut, keep all your documents ready
 masalan, ID number, Debit / Credit Card number yaa netbanking number
 Try to remember all these numbers so that time is not wasted
 6
 Try 2nd AC first: If you are cutting AC ticket then try 2nd AC first
 kyonki zyaadaatar root par 2AC kii tulana main 3AC zyada teji se bharta he
 In this case, the chances of getting tickets in 2AC are increased
 waisi trainon main tatkaal tikat kataane kii bilkul koshish naa karen jisamen tikat milane kii sambhaavna kam ho
 7
 pement ke liye hameshaa netbanking kaa istemaal karen:ye sunakar aapako thodaa ajeeb lag saktaa he lekin ye sach he ki Debit / Credit Card kii tulana main netbanking main pement zyada teji se hota he
 Because in Debit / Credit card you have to fill the card number and the other details
 lekin netbanking main aisa kuch nahin karnaa padataa
 Payment Always use the payment gateway of HDFC / ICICI
 ye baaki getwe se zyada teji se process hota he
 So here are some tips that can help you get confirmed Tatkal tickets
 dua he in tips kii madad se aap is saal holi main apane parivaar or doston ke saath apane ghar par maujuud rahen
 The rest is Happy Holi
